00328     // connecte le widget dial_buttons √  la fen√™tre de configuration

00331     connect( dial_buttons, SIGNAL(accepted()), settings_window, SLOT(accept()) );
00332     // Cliquer sur le boutton Cancel dans cette fen√™tre emet un signet rejected() qui est re√ßu par la fen√™tre de configuration.

00334     connect( dial_buttons, SIGNAL(rejected()), settings_window, SLOT(reject()) );

01471 
01472 void ImageViewer::print()
01473 {
01474     Q_ASSERT(&(imageLabel->get_qimage()));
01475 #ifndef QT_NO_PRINTER
01476     QPrintDialog dialog(&printer, this);
01477     if( dialog.exec() ) {
01478         QPainter painter(&printer);
01479         QRect rect = painter.viewport();
01480         QSize size = (&(imageLabel->get_qimage()))->size();
01481         size.scale(rect.size(), Qt::KeepAspectRatio);
01482         painter.setViewport(rect.x(), rect.y(), size.width(), size.height());
01483         painter.setWindow((&(imageLabel->get_qimage()))->rect());
01484         painter.drawImage(0, 0, *(&(imageLabel->get_qimage())));
01485     }
01486 #endif
01487 }

01509 void ImageViewer::start()
01510 {
01511 
01512     startAct->setEnabled(false);
01513     openAct->setEnabled(false);
01514     stopAct->setEnabled(true);
01515 
01516     // variables pour les √©venements clic droit et clic gauche de la souris
01517     hasClickStopping = false;
01518 
01519     if( img1 != NULL || img1_rgb != NULL ) {
01520 
01521         // Filtre
01522 
01523         // cr√©ation objet en statique
01524         //Filters filters1(img1, img_height, img_width);
01525 
01526         // cr√©ation objet dynamique (permet de recup√©rer filtered depuis la fonction MouseMooveEvent)
01527         // evite copie d'un buffer
01528         if( filters1 != NULL ) {
01529             delete filters1;
01530             filters1 = NULL;
01531         }
01532 
01533         if( filtersRGB1 != NULL ) {
01534             delete filtersRGB1;
01535             filtersRGB1 = NULL;
01536         }
01537 
01538         const unsigned char* img1_filtered;
01539         const unsigned int* img1_filtered_rgb;
01540 
01541         if( !isRgb1 ) {
01542 
01543             filters1 = new ofeli::Filters(img1, img_width, img_height);
01544 
01545             if( hasPreprocess ) {
01546 
01547                 if( hasGaussianNoise ) {
01548                     filters1->gaussian_white_noise(std_noise);
01549                 }
01550                 if( hasSaltNoise ) {
01551                     filters1->salt_pepper_noise(proba_noise);
01552                 }
01553                 if( hasSpeckleNoise ) {
01554                     filters1->speckle(std_speckle_noise);
01555                 }
01556 
01557                 if( hasMeanFilt ) {
01558                     filters1->mean_filtering(kernel_mean_length1);
01559                 }
01560                 if( hasGaussianFilt ) {
01561                     filters1->gaussian_filtering(kernel_gaussian_length1, sigma);
01562                 }
01563 
01564                 if( hasMedianFilt ) {
01565                     if( hasO1algo1 ) {
01566                         filters1->median_filtering_o1(kernel_median_length1);
01567                     }
01568                     else {
01569                         filters1->median_filtering_oNlogN(kernel_median_length1);
01570                     }
01571                 }
01572                 if( hasAnisoDiff ) {
01573                     filters1->anisotropic_diffusion(max_itera1, lambda1, kappa1, aniso_option1);
01574                 }  
01575                 if( hasOpenFilt ) {
01576                     if( hasO1morpho1 ) {
01577                         filters1->opening_o1(kernel_open_length1);
01578                     }
01579                     else {
01580                         filters1->opening(kernel_open_length1);
01581                     }
01582                 }
01583                 if( hasCloseFilt ) {
01584                     if( hasO1morpho1 ) {
01585                         filters1->closing_o1(kernel_close_length1);
01586                     }
01587                     else {
01588                         filters1->closing(kernel_close_length1);
01589                     }
01590                 }
01591                 if( hasTophatFilt ) {
01592                     if( isWhiteTophat ) {
01593                         if( hasO1morpho1 ) {
01594                             filters1->white_top_hat_o1(kernel_tophat_length1);
01595                         }
01596                         else {
01597                             filters1->white_top_hat(kernel_tophat_length1);
01598                         }
01599                     }
01600                     else {
01601                         if( hasO1morpho1 ) {
01602                             filters1->black_top_hat_o1(kernel_tophat_length1);
01603                         }
01604                         else {
01605                             filters1->black_top_hat(kernel_tophat_length1);
01606                         }
01607                     }
01608                 }
01609 
01610             }
01611 
01612             if( model == 2 ) {
01613                 filters1->morphological_gradient(kernel_gradient_length1);
01614             }
01615 
01616             img1_filtered = filters1->get_filtered();
01617 
01618         }
01619 
01620         else {
01621 
01622             filtersRGB1 = new ofeli::FiltersRGB(img1_rgb, img_width, img_height);

02243                             image_result_uchar[3*i] = I;
02244                             image_result_uchar[3*i+1] = I;
02245                             image_result_uchar[3*i+2] = I;
02246                         }
02247 
02248                     }
02249 
02250                 }
02251 
02252                 else {
02253 
02254                     for( std::list<int>::const_iterator itera = Lout1.begin(); itera != Lout1.end(); ++itera ) {
02255 
02256                         i = *itera;
02257 
02258                         RGB_uint = img1_filtered_rgb[i];
02259 
02260                         image_result_uchar[3*i] = getR(RGB_uint);
02261                         image_result_uchar[3*i+1] = getG(RGB_uint);
02262                         image_result_uchar[3*i+2] = getB(RGB_uint);
02263                     }
02264 
02265                     for( std::list<int>::const_iterator itera = Lin1.begin(); itera != Lin1.end(); ++itera ) {
02266 
02267                         i = *itera;
02268 
02269                         RGB_uint = img1_filtered_rgb[i];
02270 
02271                         image_result_uchar[3*i] = getR(RGB_uint);
02272                         image_result_uchar[3*i+1] = getG(RGB_uint);
02273                         image_result_uchar[3*i+2] = getB(RGB_uint);
02274                     }
02275                 }
02276 
02277                 if( model == 1 ) {
02278                     if( !isRgb1 ) {
02279                         acWithoutEdges1->evolve_one_iteration();
02280                         Lout1 = acWithoutEdges1->get_Lout();
02281                         Lin1 = acWithoutEdges1->get_Lin();
02282 
02283                         iterations1 = acWithoutEdges1->get_iterations();
02284                         hasAlgoStopping1 = acWithoutEdges1->get_hasAlgoStopping();
02285 
02286                         // pour l'affichage
02287                         Cout1 = acWithoutEdges1->get_Cout();
02288                         Cin1 = acWithoutEdges1->get_Cin();
02289                         RGBout = QColor(Cout1,Cout1,Cout1);
02290                         RGBin = QColor(Cin1,Cin1,Cin1);
02291                         Cout_text->setText(Cout_str+"<font color="+RGBout.name()+">"+QString::number(Cout1));
02292                         Cin_text->setText(Cin_str+"<font color="+RGBin.name()+">"+QString::number(Cin1));
02293                     }
02294                     else {
02295                         acWithoutEdgesYUV1->evolve_one_iteration();
02296                         Lout1 = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_Lout();
02297                         Lin1 = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_Lin();
02298 
02299                         iterations1 = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_iterations();
02300                         hasAlgoStopping1 = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_hasAlgoStopping();
02301 
02302                         CoutY1 = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_CoutY();
02303                         CinY1 = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_CinY();
02304                         CoutU1 = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_CoutU();
02305                         CinU1 = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_CinU();
02306                         CoutV1 = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_CoutV();
02307                         CinV1 = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_CinV();
02308 
02309                         CoutR = (unsigned char) (double(CoutY1) +1.13983 * (double(CoutV1)*1.23-0.615*255.0));
02310                         CoutG = (unsigned char) (double(CoutY1) -0.39465 * (double(CoutU1)*0.872-0.436*255.0) -0.58060 * (double(CoutV1)*1.23-0.615*255.0));
02311                         CoutB = (unsigned char) (double(CoutY1) +2.03211 * (double(CoutU1)*0.872-0.436*255.0));
02312 
02313                         CinR = (unsigned char) (double(CinY1) +1.13983 * (double(CinV1)*1.23-0.615*255.0));
02314                         CinG = (unsigned char) (double(CinY1) -0.39465 * (double(CinU1)*0.872-0.436*255.0) -0.58060 * (double(CinV1)*1.23-0.615*255.0));
02315                         CinB = (unsigned char) (double(CinY1) +2.03211 * (double(CinU1)*0.872-0.436*255.0));
02316 
02317                         RGBout = QColor(CoutR,CoutG,CoutB);
02318                         RGBin = QColor(CinR,CinG,CinB);
02319 
02320                         Cout_text->setText(Cout_str+"<font color="+RGBout.name()+">"+"("+QString::number(CoutY1)+","+QString::number(CoutU1)+","+QString::number(CoutV1)+")");
02321                         Cin_text->setText(Cin_str+"<font color="+RGBin.name()+">"+"("+QString::number(CinY1)+","+QString::number(CinU1)+","+QString::number(CinV1)+")");
02322                     }
02323                 }
02324                 if( model == 2 ) {
02325                     geodesicAc1->evolve_one_iteration();
02326                     Lout1 = geodesicAc1->get_Lout();
02327                     Lin1 = geodesicAc1->get_Lin();
02328 
02329                     iterations1 = geodesicAc1->get_iterations();
02330                     hasAlgoStopping1 = geodesicAc1->get_hasAlgoStopping();
02331                     // pour l'affichage
02332                     otsu_threshold1 = geodesicAc1->get_otsu_threshold();
02333                     threshold_text->setText(tr("Otsu's threshold of gradient = ")+QString::number(otsu_threshold1));
02334                 }
02335 
02336                 text->setText("<font color=green>"+tr("iterations (‚â§")+QString::number(max_iterations1)+") = "+QString::number(iterations1));
02337 
02338                 // marque les contours dans la QImage
02339                 for( std::list<int>::const_iterator itera = Lout1.begin(); itera != Lout1.end(); ++itera ) {
02340 
02341                     i = *itera*3;
02342 
02343                     image_result_uchar[i] = Rout1;
02344                     image_result_uchar[i+1] = Gout1;
02345                     image_result_uchar[i+2] = Bout1;
02346                 }
02347 
02348                 for( std::list<int>::const_iterator itera = Lin1.begin(); itera != Lin1.end(); ++itera ) {
02349 
02350                     i = *itera*3;
02351 
02352                     image_result_uchar[i] = Rin1;
02353                     image_result_uchar[i+1] = Gin1;
02354                     image_result_uchar[i+2] = Bin1;
02355 
02356                 }
02357 
02358                 // Pour afficher plusieurs fois dans une boucle
02359                 QApplication::processEvents();
02360                 // Affichage
02361                 //imageLabel->set_qimage(image_result);
02362                 imageLabel->update();
02363                 infinite_loop();
02364             } while (!hasAlgoStopping1);
02365 
02366             // Temps d'ex√©cution de la boucle do-while
02367             stopTime = clock();
02368             elapsedTime = (stopTime - startTime) / double(CLOCKS_PER_SEC);
02369             for( int z = 0; z < 200; z++ ) {
02370                 QApplication::processEvents();
02371                 time_text->setText(tr("time = ")+QString::number(elapsedTime)+" s");
02372             }
02373 
02374         }
02375         // on affiche rien du tout pour evaluer le temps de calcul
02376         // if (!hasDisplayEach)
02377         else {
02378             // Pour calculer le temps d'ex√©cution
02379             double elapsedTime;
02380             clock_t stopTime, startTime;
02381 
02382             startTime = clock();
02383 
02384             if( model == 1 ) {
02385                 if( !isRgb1 ) {
02386                     acWithoutEdges1->evolve_to_final_state();
02387                     Lout1 = acWithoutEdges1->get_Lout();
02388                     Lin1 = acWithoutEdges1->get_Lin();
02389                 }
02390                 else {
02391                     acWithoutEdgesYUV1->evolve_to_final_state();
02392                     Lout1 = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_Lout();
02393                     Lin1 = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_Lin();
02394                 }
02395             }
02396             if( model == 2 ) {
02397                 geodesicAc1->evolve_to_final_state();
02398                 Lout1 = geodesicAc1->get_Lout();
02399                 Lin1 = geodesicAc1->get_Lin();
02400             }
02401 
02402             // Temps d'ex√©cution de la boucle do-while
02403             stopTime = clock();
02404             elapsedTime = (stopTime - startTime) / double(CLOCKS_PER_SEC);
02405             for( int z = 0; z < 200; z++ ) {
02406                 QApplication::processEvents();
02407                 time_text->setText(tr("time = ")+QString::number(elapsedTime)+" s");
02408             }
02409         }
02410 
02411         if( model == 1 ) {
02412             if( !isRgb1 ) {
02413                 iterations1 = acWithoutEdges1->get_iterations();
02414                 hasListsChanges1 = acWithoutEdges1->get_hasListsChanges();
02415                 hasOscillation1 = acWithoutEdges1->get_hasOscillation();
02416 
02417                 Cout1 = acWithoutEdges1->get_Cout();
02418                 Cin1 = acWithoutEdges1->get_Cin();
02419                 RGBout = QColor(Cout1,Cout1,Cout1);
02420                 RGBin = QColor(Cin1,Cin1,Cin1);
02421                 Cout_text->setText(Cout_str+"<font color="+RGBout.name()+">"+QString::number(Cout1));
02422                 Cin_text->setText(Cin_str+"<font color="+RGBin.name()+">"+QString::number(Cin1));
02423             }
02424             else {
02425                 iterations1 = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_iterations();
02426                 hasListsChanges1 = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_hasListsChanges();
02427                 hasOscillation1 = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_hasOscillation();
02428 
02429                 CoutY1 = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_CoutY();
02430                 CinY1 = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_CinY();
02431                 CoutU1 = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_CoutU();
02432                 CinU1 = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_CinU();
02433                 CoutV1 = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_CoutV();
02434                 CinV1 = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_CinV();
02435 
02436                 CoutR = (unsigned char) (double(CoutY1) +1.13983 * (double(CoutV1)*1.23-0.615*255.0));
02437                 CoutG = (unsigned char) (double(CoutY1) -0.39465 * (double(CoutU1)*0.872-0.436*255.0) -0.58060 * (double(CoutV1)*1.23-0.615*255.0));
02438                 CoutB = (unsigned char) (double(CoutY1) +2.03211 * (double(CoutU1)*0.872-0.436*255.0));
02439 
02440                 CinR = (unsigned char) (double(CinY1) +1.13983 * (double(CinV1)*1.23-0.615*255.0));
02441                 CinG = (unsigned char) (double(CinY1) -0.39465 * (double(CinU1)*0.872-0.436*255.0) -0.58060 * (double(CinV1)*1.23-0.615*255.0));
02442                 CinB = (unsigned char) (double(CinY1) +2.03211 * (double(CinU1)*0.872-0.436*255.0));
02443 
02444                 RGBout = QColor(CoutR,CoutG,CoutB);
02445                 RGBin = QColor(CinR,CinG,CinB);
02446 
02447                 Cout_text->setText(Cout_str+"<font color="+RGBout.name()+">"+"("+QString::number(CoutY1)+","+QString::number(CoutU1)+","+QString::number(CoutV1)+")");
02448                 Cin_text->setText(Cin_str+"<font color="+RGBin.name()+">"+"("+QString::number(CinY1)+","+QString::number(CinU1)+","+QString::number(CinV1)+")");
02449             }
02450         }
02451         if( model == 2 ) {
02452             iterations1 = geodesicAc1->get_iterations();
02453             hasListsChanges1 = geodesicAc1->get_hasListsChanges();
02454             hasOscillation1 = geodesicAc1->get_hasOscillation();
02455         }
02456 
02457 
02458         for( int z = 0; z < 200; z++ ) {
02459             QApplication::processEvents();
02460             if( !hasListsChanges1 ) {
02461                 changes_text->setText("<font color=red>"+tr("lists changes = false"));
02462             }
02463 
02464             if( hasOscillation1 ) {
02465                 oscillation_text->setText("<font color=red>"+tr("oscillation = true"));
02466             }
02467 
02468             if( iterations1 >= max_iterations1 ) {
02469                 text->setText("<font color=red>"+tr("iterations (‚â§")+QString::number(max_iterations1)+") = "+QString::number(iterations1));
02470             }
02471             else {
02472                 text->setText("<font color=green>"+tr("iterations (‚â§")+QString::number(max_iterations1)+") = "+QString::number(iterations1));
02473             }
02474         }
02475 
02476         wait(seconds_wait/2.0);
02477         if( hasStepByStep ) {
02478             hasClickStopping = true;
02479         }
02480         infinite_loop();
02481 
02483         // affiche une fois le contour actif avec l'image initiale en dessous
02485 
02486         if( hasAlgoBreaking ) {
02487             hasAlgoBreaking = false;
02488             startAct->setEnabled(true);
02489             openAct->setEnabled(true);
02490             stopAct->setEnabled(false);
02491             return;
02492         }
02493 
02494         // marque les contours
02495         for( std::list<int>::const_iterator itera = Lout1.begin(); itera != Lout1.end(); ++itera ) {
02496 
02497             i = *itera*3;
02498 
02499             image_uchar[i] = Rout1;
02500             image_uchar[i+1] = Gout1;
02501             image_uchar[i+2] = Bout1;
02502         }
02503 
02504         for( std::list<int>::const_iterator itera = Lin1.begin(); itera != Lin1.end(); ++itera ) {
02505 
02506             i = *itera*3;
02507 
02508             image_uchar[i] = Rin1;
02509             image_uchar[i+1] = Gin1;
02510             image_uchar[i+2] = Bin1;
02511         }
02512 
02513         image_disp = 1;
02514 
02515         // Affichage
02516         imageLabel->set_qimage(image);
02517 
02519         // fin de
02521 
02522         hasResultDisp = true;
02523 
02524         openAct->setEnabled(true);
02525 
02526     }
02527     hasStepByStep = false;
02528     startAct->setEnabled(true);
02529     stopAct->setEnabled(false);
02530 
02531 }
02532 
02533 void ImageViewer::wait ( double seconds )
02534 {
02535   QApplication::processEvents();
02536 
02537   clock_t endwait;
02538   endwait = clock () + seconds * CLOCKS_PER_SEC ;
02539   while (clock() < endwait) {}
02540 }

02669 
02671 void ImageViewer::scaleImage(double factor)
02672 {
02673     Q_ASSERT(imageLabel->pixmap());
02674     scaleFactor *= factor;
02675     imageLabel->resize(scaleFactor * imageLabel->pixmap()->size());
02676 
02677     // ajout de code, pour r√©cuperer les infos lors d'un zoom pour la segmentation
02679 
02680     adjustScrollBar(scrollArea->horizontalScrollBar(), factor);
02681     adjustScrollBar(scrollArea->verticalScrollBar(), factor);
02682 
02683     zoomInAct->setEnabled(scaleFactor < 3.0);
02684     zoomOutAct->setEnabled(scaleFactor > 0.333);
02685 }
02686 
02687 void ImageViewer::adjustScrollBar(QScrollBar *scrollBar, double factor)
02688 {
02689     scrollBar->setValue(int(factor * scrollBar->value()
02690                             + ((factor - 1) * scrollBar->pageStep()/2)));
02691 }

02700 
02702 QVBoxLayout *ImageViewer::algorithm()
02703 {
02704 
02705     // cr√©ation de 3 groupbox pour l'onglet algorithm
02706 
02709 
02710     QGroupBox* externalspeed_groupbox = new QGroupBox(tr("Cycle 1 : data dependant evolution"));
02711 
02712     Na_spin = new QSpinBox;
02713     Na_spin->setSingleStep(1);
02714     Na_spin->setMinimum(1);
02715     Na_spin->setMaximum(999);
02716     Na_spin->setSuffix(tr(" iterations"));
02717     Na_spin->setToolTip(tr("iterations in the cycle 1, active contour penetrability"));
02718     QFormLayout *Na_layout = new QFormLayout;
02719     Na_layout->addRow("Na =", Na_spin);
02720     if( operating_system == 2 ) {
02721         Na_layout->setFormAlignment(Qt::AlignLeft);
02722     }
02723 
02724     klength_gradient_spin = new QSpinBox;
02725     klength_gradient_spin->setSingleStep(2);
02726     klength_gradient_spin->setMinimum(1);
02727     klength_gradient_spin->setMaximum(499);
02728 
02729     chanvese_radio = new QRadioButton(tr("Chan-Vese model"));
02730     chanvese_radio->setToolTip(tr("region-based model for bimodal images"));
02731 
02732     lambda_out_spin = new QSpinBox;
02733     lambda_out_spin->setSingleStep(1);
02734     lambda_out_spin->setMinimum(0);
02735     lambda_out_spin->setMaximum(100000);
02736     lambda_out_spin->setToolTip(tr("weight of the outside homogeneity criterion"));
02737 
02738     lambda_in_spin = new QSpinBox;
02739     lambda_in_spin->setSingleStep(1);
02740     lambda_in_spin->setMinimum(0);
02741     lambda_in_spin->setMaximum(100000);
02742     lambda_in_spin->setToolTip(tr("weight of the inside homogeneity criterion"));
02743 
02744     QFormLayout* lambda_layout = new QFormLayout;
02745     QColor RGBout_list(Rout2,Gout2,Bout2);
02746     QColor RGBin_list(Rin2,Gin2,Bin2);
02747     lambda_layout->addRow("<font color="+RGBout_list.name()+">"+"Œªout =", lambda_out_spin);
02748     lambda_layout->addRow("<font color="+RGBin_list.name()+">"+"Œªin =", lambda_in_spin);
02749     if( operating_system == 2 ) {
02750         lambda_layout->setFormAlignment(Qt::AlignLeft);
02751     }
02752 
02753     QVBoxLayout* chanvese_layout = new QVBoxLayout;
02754     chanvese_layout->addWidget(chanvese_radio);
02755     chanvese_layout->addLayout(lambda_layout);
02756 
02757     geodesic_radio = new QRadioButton(tr("geodesic model"));
02758     geodesic_radio->setToolTip(tr("edge-based model for smoothed multimodal images"));
02759 
02760     klength_gradient_spin = new QSpinBox;
02761     klength_gradient_spin->setSingleStep(2);
02762     klength_gradient_spin->setMinimum(1);
02763     klength_gradient_spin->setMaximum(499);
02764     klength_gradient_spin->setSuffix("¬≤");
02765     klength_gradient_spin->setToolTip(tr("morphological gradient structuring element size"));
02766     QFormLayout *gradient_layout = new QFormLayout;
02767     gradient_layout->addRow(tr("SE size ="), klength_gradient_spin);
02768     if( operating_system == 2 ) {
02769         gradient_layout->setFormAlignment(Qt::AlignLeft);
02770     }
02771     connect(klength_gradient_spin,SIGNAL(valueChanged(int)),this,SLOT(filtering_visu()));
02772 
02773     QVBoxLayout* geodesic_layout = new QVBoxLayout;
02774     geodesic_layout->addWidget(geodesic_radio);
02775     geodesic_layout->addLayout(gradient_layout);
02776 
02777     QHBoxLayout* speed_layout = new QHBoxLayout;
02778     speed_layout->addLayout(chanvese_layout);
02779     speed_layout->addLayout(geodesic_layout);
02780 
02781     yuv_groupbox = new QGroupBox(tr("normalized (Y,U,V) color space weighting"));
02782     yuv_groupbox->setFlat(true);
02783 
02784     Yspin = new QSpinBox;

03565 
03566 
03568 void ImageViewer::settings()
03569 {
03570 
03571     if( onglets->currentIndex() == 1 ) {
03572         filtering_visu();
03573         phi_visu(true);
03574         shape_visu();
03575     }
03576     else {
03577         filtering_visu();
03578         phi_visu(false);
03579     }
03580 
03581     // on s'assure que la fen√™tre de configuration n'est pas d√©ja affich√©e
03582     if( settings_window->isVisible() ) {
03583         QMessageBox::critical(this, tr("Error"), tr("Close settings window before."));
03584     }
03585     else {
03586 
03587         // bool√©en permettant de savoir si l'utilisateur accepte ou rejette les r√©glages de la fen√™tre de configuration
03588         int result_settings_window;
03589 
03590         // la m√©thode exec() permet d'afficher la fen√™tre de configuration settings_window de maniere modale,
03591         // de plus cette m√©thode retourne un bool√©en en fonction de l'acceptation ou du rejet des r√©glages
03592         result_settings_window = settings_window->exec();
03593 
03594         // la m√©thode show() permet d'afficher la fen√™tre de configuration mais de maniere non modale,
03595         //  ne renvoie pas de bool√©en
03596         //settings_window->show();
03597 
03598         if( result_settings_window ) {
03599             // Ok = les variables vont prendre leur valeur en fonction de l'√©tat des widgets de la fen√™tre de configuration
03600             apply_settings();
03601 
03602         }
03603         else {
03604             // Annuler = les widgets vont reprendre leur √©tat en fonction des valeurs des variables
03605             cancel_settings();
03606         }
03607 
03608     }
03609 }
03610 
03613 void ImageViewer::apply_settings() {
03614 
03615     // affection des variables en fonction des √©tats des widgets
03616 
03618     //          Algorithm            //
03620 
03621     Na1 = Na_spin->value();
03622 
03623     if( chanvese_radio->isChecked() ) {
03624         model = 1;
03625     }
03626     if( geodesic_radio->isChecked() ) {
03627         model = 2;
03628     }
03629 
03630     lambda_out1 = lambda_out_spin->value();
03631     lambda_in1 = lambda_in_spin->value();
03632 
03633     kernel_gradient_length1 = klength_gradient_spin->value();
03634 
03635     alpha1 = Yspin->value();
03636     beta1 = Uspin->value();
03637     gamma1 = Vspin->value();
03638 
03639     if( internalspeed_groupbox->isChecked() ) {
03640         hasSmoothingCycle1 = true;
03641     }
03642     else {
03643         hasSmoothingCycle1 = false;
03644     }
03645 
03646     Ns1 = Ns_spin->value();
03647 
03648     kernel_curve1 = klength_spin->value();
03649     std_curve1 = std_spin->value();
03650 
03651     if( cleanbound_checkbox->isChecked() ) {
03652         hasCleaning1 = true;
03653     }
03654     else {
03655         hasCleaning1 = false;
03656     }
03657 
03659     //       Initialization          //
03661 
03662     if( rectangle_radio->isChecked() ) {
03663         hasEllipse1 = false;
03664     }
03665     if( ellipse_radio->isChecked() ) {
03666         hasEllipse1 = true;
03667     }
03668 
03669     init_width1 = double(width_shape_spin->value())/100.0;
03670     init_height1 = double(height_shape_spin->value())/100.0;
03671

03674 
03676     //        Preprocessing          //
03678

03680         hasPreprocess = true;
03681     }
03682     else {
03683         hasPreprocess = false;
03684     }
03685

03687         hasGaussianNoise = true;
03688     }
03689     else {
03690         hasGaussianNoise = false;

03695         hasSaltNoise = true;
03696     }
03697     else {
03698         hasSaltNoise = false;
03699     }
03700     proba_noise = proba_noise_spin->value()/100.0;

03704     }
03705     else {
03706         hasSpeckleNoise = false;
03707     }
03708     std_speckle_noise = std_speckle_noise_spin->value();
03709

03712     }
03713     else {
03714         hasMedianFilt = false;
03715     }
03716     kernel_median_length1 = klength_median_spin->value();
03717     if( complex_radio2->isChecked() ) {

03719     }
03720     else {

03722     }
03723

03725         hasMeanFilt = true;
03726     }
03727     else {
03728         hasMeanFilt = false;
03729     }
03730     kernel_mean_length1 = klength_mean_spin->value();
03731 
03732     if( gaussian_groupbox->isChecked() ) {
03733         hasGaussianFilt = true;
03734     }
03735     else {
03736         hasGaussianFilt = false;
03737     }
03738     kernel_gaussian_length1 = klength_gaussian_spin->value();
03739     sigma = std_filter_spin->value();
03740

03743     }

03746     }

03760     }
03761     else {
03762         hasOpenFilt = false;
03763     }

03765

03768     }

04519     Gin_selected1 = 128;
04520     Bin_selected1 = 0;
04521 
04522     seconds_wait = 1.0;
04523 
04524     hasEllipse1 = true;
04525     init_width1 = 0.65;
04526     init_height1 = 0.65;
04527     center_x1 = 0.0;
04528     center_y1 = 0.0;
04529     cancel_settings();
04530 
04531     scale_spin->setValue(100);
04532 
04533     QImage img_phi0 = QImage(100,100, QImage::Format_RGB888);
04534 
04535 
04536     int i; // offset
04537 
04538     int x; // column index or X-axis position
04539     int y; // row index or Y-axis position
04540 
04541     for( i = 0; i < 10000; i++ ) {
04542 
04543         // i = x+y*img_width so
04544         y = i/100;
04545         x = i-y*100;
04546 
04547         if( x < 95 && x > 5 && y < 95 && y > 5 ) {
04548             img_phi0.setPixel(x,y,qRgb(255,255,255));
04549         }
04550         else {
04551             img_phi0.setPixel(x,y,qRgb(0,0,0));
04552         }
04553 
04554     }
04555 
04556     img_phi = img_phi0.scaled( img_width, img_height, Qt::IgnoreAspectRatio, Qt::SmoothTransformation);
04557 
04558     imgPhi2phiInit();
04559 
04560     // pour afficher l'image dans la fenetre settings
04561     Lout2.clear();
04562     Lin2.clear();
04563     Lout_shape.clear();
04564     Lin_shape.clear();
04565 
04566     for( i = 0; i < size1; i++ ) {
04567         if( phi_init1_clean[i] == -1 ) {
04568             Lin2.push_front(i);
04569         }
04570         if( phi_init1_clean[i] == 1 ) {
04571             Lout2.push_front(i);
04572         }
04573     }
04574     filtering_visu();
04575     tab_visu(onglets->currentIndex());
04576 
04577 }

04593 inline void ImageViewer::clean_boundaries(char* phi, char* phi_clean) {
04594 
04595     if( phi != NULL && phi_clean != NULL ) {
04596 
04597         int i; // offset
04598 
04599         int x; // column index or X-axis position
04600         int y; // row index or Y-axis position
04601 
04602         for( i = 0; i < size1; i++ ) {
04603 
04604             if( phi[i] == 1 ) {
04605 
04606                 // i = x+y*img_width so
04607                 y = i/img_width;
04608                 x = i-y*img_width;
04609 
04610                 // nettoyage si la condition de voisinage aux fronti√®res n'est pas respect√©e
04611                 if( isRedundantPointOfLout(phi,x,y) ) {
04612                     phi_clean[i] = 3;
04613                 }
04614                 else {
04615                     phi_clean[i] = 1;
04616                 }
04617             }
04618 
04619             if( phi[i] == -1 ) {
04620 
04621                 // i = x+y*img_width so
04622                 y = i/img_width;
04623                 x = i-y*img_width;
04624 
04625                 if( isRedundantPointOfLin(phi,x,y) ) {
04626                     phi_clean[i] = -3;
04627                 }
04628                 else {
04629                     phi_clean[i] = -1;
04630                 }
04631             }
04632         }
04633 
04634         // efface l'affichage des listes
04635         for( std::list<int>::const_iterator itera = Lin2.begin(); itera != Lin2.end(); ++itera ) {
04636 
04637             i = *itera*3;
04638 
04639             image_phi_uchar[i] = image_filter_uchar[i];
04640             image_phi_uchar[i+1] = image_filter_uchar[i+1];
04641             image_phi_uchar[i+2] = image_filter_uchar[i+2];
04642 
04643             image_shape_uchar[i] = image_filter_uchar[i];
04644             image_shape_uchar[i+1] = image_filter_uchar[i+1];
04645             image_shape_uchar[i+2] = image_filter_uchar[i+2];
04646         }
04647 
04648         for( std::list<int>::const_iterator itera = Lout2.begin(); itera != Lout2.end(); ++itera ) {
04649 
04650             i = *itera*3;
04651 
04652             image_phi_uchar[i] = image_filter_uchar[i];
04653             image_phi_uchar[i+1] = image_filter_uchar[i+1];
04654             image_phi_uchar[i+2] = image_filter_uchar[i+2];
04655 
04656             image_shape_uchar[i] = image_filter_uchar[i];
04657             image_shape_uchar[i+1] = image_filter_uchar[i+1];
04658             image_shape_uchar[i+2] = image_filter_uchar[i+2];
04659         }
04660 
04661         Lout2.clear();
04662         Lin2.clear();
04663 
04664         for( i = 0; i < size1; i++ ) {
04665             if( phi_clean[i] == -1 ) {
04666                 Lin2.push_front(i);
04667             }
04668             if( phi_clean[i] == 1 ) {
04669                 Lout2.push_front(i);
04670             }
04671         }
04672     }
04673     return;
04674 }
04675 
04676 inline bool ImageViewer::isRedundantPointOfLin(char* phi, int x, int y) {
04677 
04678     // si pas sur le bord, pas de tests d'existence de voisins
04679     if( x > 0 && x < img_width-1 && y > 0 && y < img_height-1 ) {
04680 
04681         for( int dy = -1; dy <= 1; dy++ ) {
04682             for( int dx = -1; dx <= 1; dx++ ) {
04683                 if( !(dx == 0 && dy == 0) ) {
04684                     if( phi[ (x+dx)+(y+dy)*img_width ] >= 0 ) {
04685                         return false;
04686                     }
04687                 }
04688             }
04689         }
04690 
04691     }
04692 
04693     // si sur le bord, tests d'existence de voisins
04694     else {
04695 
04696         for( int dy = -1; dy <= 1; dy++ ) {
04697             for( int dx = -1; dx <= 1; dx++ ) {
04698                 if( !(dx == 0 && dy == 0) ) {
04699                     if( x+dx >= 0 && x+dx < img_width && y+dy >= 0 && y+dy < img_height ) {
04700                         if( phi[ (x+dx)+(y+dy)*img_width ] >= 0 ) {
04701                             return false;
04702                         }
04703                     }
04704                 }
04705             }
04706         }
04707 
04708     }
04709 
04710     return true;
04711 }
04712 
04713 // Fonction cr√©ee pour utiliser plusieurs return et sortir le plus t√¥t possible quand le test est faux
04714 // permet contrairement √  l'instruction break de sortir de toutes les sous-boucles d'un coup
04715 inline bool ImageViewer::isRedundantPointOfLout(char* phi, int x, int y) {
04716 
04717     // si pas sur le bord, pas de tests d'existence de voisins
04718     if( x > 0 && x < img_width-1 && y > 0 && y < img_height-1 ) {
04719 
04720         for( int dy = -1; dy <= 1; dy++ ) {
04721             for( int dx = -1; dx <= 1; dx++ ) {
04722                 if( !(dx == 0 && dy == 0) ) {
04723                     if( phi[ (x+dx)+(y+dy)*img_width ] <= 0 ) {
04724                         return false;
04725                     }
04726                 }
04727             }
04728         }
04729 
04730     }
04731 
04732     // si sur le bord, tests d'existence de voisins
04733     else {
04734 
04735         for( int dy = -1; dy <= 1; dy++ ) {
04736             for( int dx = -1; dx <= 1; dx++ ) {
04737                 if( !(dx == 0 && dy == 0) ) {
04738                     if( x+dx >= 0 && x+dx < img_width && y+dy >= 0 && y+dy < img_height ) {
04739                         if( phi[ (x+dx)+(y+dy)*img_width ] <= 0 ) {
04740                             return false;
04741                         }
04742                     }
04743                 }
04744             }
04745         }
04746 
04747     }
04748 
04749     return true;
04750 }
04751 
04753 void ImageViewer::shape_visu() {
04754 
04755     if( shape != NULL ) {
04756 
04757         init_width2 = double(width_shape_spin->value())/100.0;
04758         init_height2 = double(height_shape_spin->value())/100.0;
04759         center_x2 = double(abscissa_spin->value())/100.0;
04760         center_y2 = double(ordinate_spin->value())/100.0;
04761 
04762         if( rectangle_radio->isChecked() ) {
04763             hasEllipse2 = false;
04764         }
04765         if( ellipse_radio->isChecked() ) {
04766             hasEllipse2 = true;
04767         }
04768 
04769 
04770         int i; // offset
04771 
04772         int x; // column index or X-axis position
04773         int y; // row index or Y-axis position
04774 
04775         // efface les listes de la QImage
04776         for( std::list<int>::const_iterator itera = Lin_shape.begin(); itera != Lin_shape.end(); ++itera ) {
04777 
04778             i = *itera*3;
04779 
04780             image_shape_uchar[i] = image_phi_uchar[i];
04781             image_shape_uchar[i+1] = image_phi_uchar[i+1];
04782             image_shape_uchar[i+2] = image_phi_uchar[i+2];
04783         }
04784 
04785         for( std::list<int>::const_iterator itera = Lout_shape.begin(); itera != Lout_shape.end(); ++itera ) {
04786 
04787             i = *itera*3;
04788 
04789             image_shape_uchar[i] = image_phi_uchar[i];
04790             image_shape_uchar[i+1] = image_phi_uchar[i+1];
04791             image_shape_uchar[i+2] = image_phi_uchar[i+2];
04792         }
04793 
04794         Lout_shape.clear();
04795         Lin_shape.clear();
04796 
04797         if( hasEllipse2 ) {
04798 
04799             for( i = 0; i < size1; i++ ) {
04800 
04801                 y = i/img_width;
04802                 x = i-y*img_width;
04803 
04804                 // in√©quation de l'ellipse
04805                 // grand axe et petit axe proportionnel √  la largeur et la hauteur de l'image
04806                 // pour une image carr√©e, l'ellipse est un cercle
04807                 // variable init_shape_size par d√©faut a 0.95 (entre 0 et 1 sinon)
04808                 if( (double(y)-(1.0+2.0*center_y2)*double(img_height)/2.0)*(double(y)-(1.0+2.0*center_y2)*double(img_height)/2.0)/(init_height2*double(img_height)/2.0*init_height2*double(img_height)/2.0)+(double(x)-(1.0+2.0*center_x2)*double(img_width)/2.0)*(double(x)-(1.0+2.0*center_x2)*double(img_width)/2.0)/(init_width2*double(img_width)/2.0*init_width2*double(img_width)/2.0) > 1.0 ) {
04809                     shape[i] = 1;
04810                 }
04811                 else {
04812                     shape[i] = -1;
04813                 }
04814             }
04815 
04816         }
04817 
04818         else {
04819 
04820             for( i = 0; i < size1; i++ ) {
04821 
04822                 y = i/img_width;
04823                 x = i-y*img_width;
04824 
04825                 // pour faire un rectangle
04826                 // largeur et hauteur du rectangle proportionnel √  la largeur et la hauteur de l'image
04827                 // pour une image carr√©e, le rectangle est un carr√©
04828                 if( double(y) > ((1.0-init_height2)*double(img_height)/2.0 + center_y2*double(img_height)) && double(y) < ((double(img_height)-(1.0-init_height2)*double(img_height)/2.0) + center_y2*double(img_height)) && double(x) > ((1.0-init_width2)*double(img_width)/2.0 + center_x2*double(img_width)) && double(x) < ((double(img_width)-(1.0-init_width2)*double(img_width)/2.0) + center_x2*double(img_width)) ) {
04829                     shape[i] = -1;
04830                 }
04831                 else {
04832                     shape[i] = 1;
04833                 }
04834             }
04835 
04836         }
04837 
04838         // affiche l'ellipse ou le rectangle
04839         for( i = 0; i < size1; i++ ) {
04840 
04841             if( shape[i] == 1 ) {
04842 
04843                 y = i/img_width;
04844                 x = i-y*img_width;
04845 
04846                 if( !isRedundantPointOfLout(shape,x,y) ) {
04847                     Lout_shape.push_front(i);
04848 
04849                     image_shape_uchar[3*i] = Rout2;
04850                     image_shape_uchar[3*i+1] = Gout2;
04851                     image_shape_uchar[3*i+2] = Bout2;
04852                 }
04853             }
04854 
04855             if( shape[i] == -1 ) {
04856 
04857                 y = i/img_width;
04858                 x = i-y*img_width;
04859 
04860                 if( !isRedundantPointOfLin(shape,x,y) ) {
04861                     Lin_shape.push_front(i);
04862                     image_shape_uchar[3*i] = Rin2;
04863                     image_shape_uchar[3*i+1] = Gin2;
04864                     image_shape_uchar[3*i+2] = Bin2;
04865                 }
04866             }
04867         }
04868 
04869         imageLabel_settings->set_qimage(image_shape);
04870     }
04871     return;
04872 }
04873 
04875 void ImageViewer::shape_visu(int value) {
04876     shape_visu();
04877 }

04881 void ImageViewer::clean_phi_visu() {
04882 
04883     if( phi_init2 != NULL && phi_init2_clean != NULL ) {
04884 
04885         clean_boundaries(phi_init2, phi_init2_clean);
04886         for( int i = 0; i < size1; i++ ) {
04887             phi_init2[i] = 1;
04888             phi_init2_clean[i] = 3;
04889         }
04890         clean_boundaries(phi_init2, phi_init2_clean);
04891 
04892         shape_visu();
04893 
04894     }

04898 void ImageViewer::phi_subtract_shape() {
04899 
04900     if( shape != NULL && phi_init2 != NULL ) {
04901 
04902         bool phi_init2_modif = false;
04903 
04904         for( int i = 0; i < size1; i++ ) {
04905             if( shape[i] == -1 && phi_init2[i] == -1 ) {
04906                 phi_init2[i] = 1;
04907                 phi_init2_modif = true;
04908             }
04909         }
04910 
04911         clean_boundaries(phi_init2, phi_init2_clean);
04912 
04913         if( !phi_init2_modif ) {
04914             phi_add_shape();
04915         }
04916 
04917     }
04918 
04919     return;
04920 }
04921 
04923 void ImageViewer::phi_add_shape() {
04924 
04925     if( shape != NULL && phi_init2 != NULL ) {
04926 
04927         bool phi_init2_modif = false;
04928 
04929         for( int i = 0; i < size1; i++ ) {
04930             if( shape[i] == -1 && phi_init2[i] == 1 ) {
04931                 phi_init2[i] = -1;
04932                 phi_init2_modif = true;
04933             }
04934         }
04935 
04936         clean_boundaries(phi_init2, phi_init2_clean);
04937 
04938         if( !phi_init2_modif ) {
04939             phi_subtract_shape();
04940         }
04941 
04942     }
04943 
04944     return;
04945 }

05172 void ImageViewer::saveImage() {
05173 
05174     QFileInfo fi(fileName);
05175     QString fileName_save;
05176 
05177     // selection du chemin √  partir d'une bo√Æte de dialogue
05178     if( iterations1 == -1 ) {
05179 
05180         fileName_save = QFileDialog::getSaveFileName(this,
05181                                                      tr("Save the image displayed by the main window"),
05182                                                      last_directory_used + "/" + fi.baseName(),
05183                                                      "PNG (*.png)");
05184     }
05185     else {
05186 
05187         if( image_disp == 1 ) {
05188 
05189             fileName_save = QFileDialog::getSaveFileName(this,
05190                                                          tr("Save the image displayed by the main window"),
05191                                                          last_directory_used + "/" + fi.baseName()+tr("_with_phi(t=")+QString::number(iterations1)+")",
05192                                                          "PNG (*.png)");
05193         }
05194         if( image_disp == 2 && (hasPreprocess || model == 2) ) {
05195 
05196             fileName_save = QFileDialog::getSaveFileName(this,
05197                                                          tr("Save the image displayed by the main window"),
05198                                                          last_directory_used + "/" + tr("preprocessed_") +fi.baseName()+tr("_with_phi(t=")+QString::number(iterations1)+")",
05199                                                          "PNG (*.png)");
05200 
05201         }
05202 
05203     }
05204 
05205     // sauvegarde
05206     QImage img_displayed=imageLabel->get_qimage();
05207     img_displayed.save(fileName_save);
05208 
05209     if( (hasPreprocess || model == 2) && !image_save_preprocess.isNull() ) {
05210 
05211         // s√©lection du chemin+nom de sauvegarde √  partir d'une bo√Æte de dialogue
05212         QString fileName_save2 = QFileDialog::getSaveFileName(this,
05213                                                               tr("Save the preprocessed image"),
05214                                                               last_directory_used + "/" + tr("preprocessed_") + fi.baseName() + ".png",
05215                                                               "PNG (*.png)");
05216 
05217         // sauvegarde
05218         image_save_preprocess.save(fileName_save2);
05219 
05220     }
05221 
05222 }

05226 void ImageViewer::color_out() {
05227 
05228     // S√©lection d'une QColor a partir d'une boite de dialogue couleur
05229     QColor color_out = QColorDialog::getColor(Qt::white, this, tr("Select Lout color"));
05230     if( color_out.isValid() ) {
05231         Rout_selected2 = (unsigned char)(color_out.red());
05232         Gout_selected2 = (unsigned char)(color_out.green());
05233         Bout_selected2 = (unsigned char)(color_out.blue());
05234 
05235         QPixmap pm(12,12);
05236         pm.fill(color_out);
05237         outsidecolor_combobox->addItem (pm, tr("Selected"));
05238         outsidecolor_combobox->removeItem (8);
05239 
05240         outsidecolor_combobox->setCurrentIndex(8);
05241     }
05242     // affichage de l'image avec la nouvelle couleur s√©lectionn√©e
05243     phi_visu(false);
05244 
05245 }

05271 void ImageViewer::filtering_visu() {
05272 
05273     if( (img1 != NULL || img1_rgb != NULL)  && (filtersd1 != NULL || filtersRGBd1 != NULL) ) {

05275         // r√©cup√©ration de tous les √©tats des widgets de l'onglet preprocessing
05276 
05277         if( preprocessing_groupbox->isChecked() ) {
05278             hasPreprocess2 = true;
05279         }
05280         else {
05281             hasPreprocess2 = false;
05282         }
05283 
05284         if( gaussian_noise_groupbox->isChecked() ) {
05285             hasGaussianNoise2 = true;
05286         }
05287         else {
05288             hasGaussianNoise2 = false;
05289         }
05290         std_noise2 = std_noise_spin->value();
05291

05293             hasSaltNoise2 = true;
05294         }
05295         else {
05296             hasSaltNoise2 = false;
05297         }
05298         proba_noise2 = proba_noise_spin->value()/100.0;
05299 
05300         if( speckle_noise_groupbox->isChecked() ) {
05301             hasSpeckleNoise2 = true;
05302         }
05303         else {
05304             hasSpeckleNoise2 = false;
05305         }
05306         std_speckle_noise2 = std_speckle_noise_spin->value();
05307 
05308         if( median_groupbox->isChecked() ) {
05309             hasMedianFilt2 = true;
05310         }
05311         else {
05312             hasMedianFilt2 = false;
05313         }
05314         kernel_median_length2 = klength_median_spin->value();
05315         if( complex_radio2->isChecked() ) {
05316             hasO1algo2 = true;
05317         }
05318         else {
05319             hasO1algo2 = false;
05320         }
05321 
05322         if( mean_groupbox->isChecked() ) {
05323             hasMeanFilt2 = true;
05324         }
05325         else {
05326             hasMeanFilt2 = false;
05327         }
05328         kernel_mean_length2 = klength_mean_spin->value();
05329 
05330         if( gaussian_groupbox->isChecked() ) {
05331             hasGaussianFilt2 = true;
05332         }
05333         else {
05334             hasGaussianFilt2 = false;
05335         }
05336         kernel_gaussian_length2 = klength_gaussian_spin->value();
05337         sigma2 = std_filter_spin->value();
05338 
05339 
05340         if( aniso_groupbox->isChecked() ) {
05341             hasAnisoDiff2 = true;
05342         }
05343         else {
05344             hasAnisoDiff2 = false;
05345         }
05346 
05347         max_itera2 = iteration_filter_spin->value();
05348         lambda2 = lambda_spin->value();
05349         kappa2 = kappa_spin->value();
05350         if( aniso1_radio->isChecked() ) {
05351             aniso_option2 = 1;
05352         }
05353         if( aniso2_radio->isChecked() ) {
05354             aniso_option2 = 2;
05355         }
05356 
05357         if( open_groupbox->isChecked() ) {
05358             hasOpenFilt2 = true;
05359         }
05360         else {
05361             hasOpenFilt2 = false;
05362         }
05363         kernel_open_length2 = klength_open_spin->value();
05364 
05365         if( close_groupbox->isChecked() ) {
05366             hasCloseFilt2 = true;
05367         }
05368         else {
05369             hasCloseFilt2 = false;
05370         }
05371         kernel_close_length2 = klength_close_spin->value();
05372 
05373         if( tophat_groupbox->isChecked() ) {
05374             hasTophatFilt2 = true;
05375         }
05376         else {
05377             hasTophatFilt2 = false;
05378         }
05379         if( whitetophat_radio->isChecked() ) {
05380             isWhiteTophat2 = true;
05381         }
05382         else {
05383             isWhiteTophat2 = false;
05384         }
05385         kernel_tophat_length2 = klength_tophat_spin->value();
05386 
05387         if( complex2_morpho_radio->isChecked() ) {
05388             hasO1morpho2 = true;
05389         }
05390         else {
05391             hasO1morpho2 = false;
05392         }
05393

05395             model2 = 1;
05396         }
05397         if( geodesic_radio->isChecked() ) {
05398             model2 = 2;
05399         }
05400         kernel_gradient_length2 = klength_gradient_spin->value();
05401 
05402         alpha2 = Yspin->value();
05403         beta2 = Uspin->value();
05404         gamma2 = Vspin->value();
05405 
05406         if( histo_checkbox->isChecked() ) {
05407             hasHistoNormaliz2 = true;
05408         }
05409         else {
05410             hasHistoNormaliz2 = false;
05411         }
05412 
05413 
05414         if( hasOpenFilt2 || hasCloseFilt2 || hasTophatFilt2 ) {
05415             algo_groupbox->setEnabled(true);
05416         }
05417         else {
05418             algo_groupbox->setEnabled(false);
05419         }
05420 
05421         if( !isRgb1 ) {
05422 
05423             // pour refiltrer √  partir de l'image de d√©part
05424             filtersd1->initialyze_filtered();
05425

05427             clock_t stopTime;
05428             clock_t startTime;
05429

05431

05433

05435                     filtersd1->gaussian_white_noise(std_noise2);
05436                 }
05437                 if( hasSaltNoise2 ) {
05438                     filtersd1->salt_pepper_noise(proba_noise2);
05439                 }
05440                 if( hasSpeckleNoise2 ) {
05441                     filtersd1->speckle(std_speckle_noise2);
05442                 }
05443

05445                     filtersd1->mean_filtering(kernel_mean_length2);
05446                 }
05447                 if( hasGaussianFilt2 ) {

05449                 }

05453                         filtersd1->median_filtering_o1(kernel_median_length2);
05454                     }

05456                         filtersd1->median_filtering_oNlogN(kernel_median_length2);
05457                     }

05460                     filtersd1->anisotropic_diffusion(max_itera2, lambda2, kappa2, aniso_option2);
05461                 }
05462

05464                     if( hasO1morpho2 ) {
05465                         filtersd1->opening_o1(kernel_open_length2);
05466                     }
05467                     else {
05468                         filtersd1->opening(kernel_open_length2);
05469                     }
05470                 }
05471 
05472                 if( hasCloseFilt2 ) {
05473                     if( hasO1morpho2 ) {
05474                         filtersd1->closing_o1(kernel_close_length2);
05475                     }
05476                     else {
05477                         filtersd1->closing(kernel_close_length2);
05478                     }
05479                 }
05480

05484                             filtersd1->white_top_hat_o1(kernel_tophat_length2);
05485                         }
05486                         else {
05487                             filtersd1->white_top_hat(kernel_tophat_length2);
05488                         }
05489                     }

05491                         if( hasO1morpho2 ) {

05493                         }
05494                         else {
05495                             filtersd1->black_top_hat(kernel_tophat_length2);
05496                         }
05497                     }
05498                 }
05499 
05500             }
05501 
05502             stopTime = clock();
05503             elapsedTime = (stopTime - startTime) / double(CLOCKS_PER_SEC);
05504             time_filt->setText(tr("time = ")+QString::number(elapsedTime)+" s");
05505 
05506             if( model2 == 2 ) {
05507                 filtersd1->morphological_gradient(kernel_gradient_length2);
05508             }
05509 
05510             const unsigned char* img1_filtered;
05511             img1_filtered = filtersd1->get_filtered();
05512 
05513             int x; // column index or X-axis position
05514             int y; // row index or Y-axis position
05515 
05516             unsigned char I;
05517 
05518             if( model2 == 2 && hasHistoNormaliz2 ) {
05519 
05520                 unsigned char max = 0;
05521                 unsigned char min = 255;
05522

05524                     if( img1_filtered[i] > max ) {
05525                         max = img1_filtered[i];
05526                     }
05527                     if( img1_filtered[i] < min ) {
05528                         min = img1_filtered[i];
05529                     }
05530                 }
05531

05533

05535

05538                     image_filter_uchar[3*i+2] = I;
05539

05542                     image_phi_uchar[3*i+2] = I;

05547                 }
05548 
05549             }
05550             else {
05551 
05552                 for( int i = 0; i < size1; i++ ) {
05553 
05554                     I = img1_filtered[i];
05555 
05556                     image_filter_uchar[3*i] = I;
05557                     image_filter_uchar[3*i+1] = I;
05558                     image_filter_uchar[3*i+2] = I;
05559 
05560                     image_phi_uchar[3*i] = I;
05561                     image_phi_uchar[3*i+1] = I;
05562                     image_phi_uchar[3*i+2] = I;

05571

05573 
05574             // pour refiltrer √  partir de l'image de d√©part
05575             filtersRGBd1->initialyze_filtered();
05576

05582

05590                 }
05591                 if( hasSpeckleNoise2 ) {
05592                     filtersRGBd1->speckle(std_speckle_noise2);

05596                     filtersRGBd1->mean_filtering(kernel_mean_length2);

05603                     if( hasO1algo2 ) {
05604                         filtersRGBd1->median_filtering_o1(kernel_median_length2);

05764 void ImageViewer::tab_visu(int value) {
05765     if( img1 != NULL || img1_rgb != NULL ) {
05766         // si onglet initilisation
05767         if( value == 1 ) {
05768             // visualisation de la forme
05769             phi_visu(true);
05770             shape_visu();
05771             imageLabel_settings->set_doWheelEvent(false);
05772         }
05773         else {
05774             // visualisation de phi
05775             phi_visu(false);
05776             imageLabel_settings->set_doWheelEvent(true);
05777         }
05778     }
05779 }
05780 
05782 void ImageViewer::mousePressEvent(QMouseEvent *event)
05783 {
05784 
05785     // si l'image est charg√©e
05786     if( img1 != NULL || img1_rgb != NULL ) {
05787 
05788         if( !startAct->isEnabled() ) {
05789 
05790             if( event->button() == Qt::LeftButton ) {
05791                 hasStepByStep = false;
05792                 hasClickStopping = true;
05793             }
05794 
05795             if( event->button() == Qt::RightButton ) {
05796                 hasClickStopping = false;
05797                 hasStepByStep = true;
05798             }
05799 
05800         }
05801 
05802         else {
05803 
05804             if( event->button() == Qt::RightButton ) {
05805                 hasStepByStep = true;
05806                 start();
05807             }
05808         }
05809 
05810     }
05811 }
05812 
05814 void ImageViewer::mouseReleaseEvent(QMouseEvent *event)
05815 {
05816 
05817     // si l'image est charg√©e
05818     if( img1 != NULL || img1_rgb != NULL ) {
05819 
05820         if( !startAct->isEnabled() ) {
05821 
05822             if( event->button() == Qt::LeftButton ) {
05823                 hasStepByStep = false;
05824                 hasClickStopping = false;
05825             }
05826         }
05827 
05828         else {
05829 
05830             if( event->button() == Qt::LeftButton ) {
05831                 start();
05832             }
05833 
05834         }
05835 
05836     }
05837 
05838 }
05839 
05841 void ImageViewer::keyPressEvent(QKeyEvent *event)
05842 {
05843 
05844     // si l'image est charg√©e
05845     if( img1 != NULL || img1_rgb != NULL ) {
05846 
05847         if( !startAct->isEnabled() ) {
05848 
05849             if( !event->isAutoRepeat() ) {
05850                 if( event->key() == Qt::Key_Space || event->key() == Qt::Key_Right || event->key() == Qt::Key_Pause ) {
05851                     hasStepByStep = false;
05852                     hasClickStopping = true;
05853                 }
05854             }
05855 
05856             if( event->key() == Qt::Key_Return || event->key() == Qt::Key_Up || event->key() == Qt::Key_Down ) {
05857                 hasClickStopping = false;
05858                 hasStepByStep = true;
05859             }
05860 
05861         }
05862 
05863         else {
05864 
05865             if( !event->isAutoRepeat() ) {
05866                 if( event->key() == Qt::Key_Return || event->key() == Qt::Key_Up || event->key() == Qt::Key_Down ) {
05867                     hasClickStopping = false;
05868                     hasStepByStep = true;
05869                     start();
05870                 }
05871             }
05872 
05873         }
05874     }
05875 }
05876 
05878 void ImageViewer::keyReleaseEvent(QKeyEvent *event)
05879 {
05880 
05881     // si l'image est charg√©e
05882     if( img1 != NULL || img1_rgb != NULL ) {
05883 
05884         if( !event->isAutoRepeat() ) {
05885 
05886             if( !startAct->isEnabled() ) {
05887 
05888                 if( event->key() == Qt::Key_Space || event->key() == Qt::Key_Right || event->key() == Qt::Key_Pause ) {
05889                     hasStepByStep = false;
05890                     hasClickStopping = false;
05891                 }
05892             }
05893             else {
05894 
05895                 if( event->key() == Qt::Key_Space || event->key() == Qt::Key_Up || event->key() == Qt::Key_Pause ) {
05896                     start();
05897                 }
05898 
05899             }
05900 
05901         }
05902 
05903     }
05904 
05905 }

05910 void ImageViewer::infinite_loop() {
05911 
05912     while( hasClickStopping ) {
05913         QApplication::processEvents();
05914     }

05918 void ImageViewer::mouseMoveEvent(QMouseEvent *event)
05919 {
05920 
05921     // si l'image est charg√©e
05922     if( img1 != NULL || img1_rgb != NULL ) {
05923 
05924         positionX = int(double(img_width)*double(   (  (event->pos()).x() -imageLabel->get_xoffset()    ) /double(imageLabel->getPixWidth())));
05925         positionY = int(double(img_height)*double(   (  (event->pos()).y() -imageLabel->get_yoffset()   ) /double(imageLabel->getPixHeight())));
05926 
05927         if( positionX >= 0 && positionX < img_width && positionY >= 0 && positionY < img_height ) {
05928 
05929             if( image_disp == 1 ) {
05930                 if( !isRgb1 ) {
05931                     int I = img1[ positionX+positionY*img_width ];
05932                     QColor RGB(I,I,I);
05933                     pixel_text->setText(tr("img(")+QString::number(positionX+1)+","+QString::number(positionY+1)+") = "+"<font color="+RGB.name()+">"+QString::number(I));
05934 
05935                 }
05936                 else {
05937                     unsigned int RGB_uint = img1_rgb[ positionX+positionY*img_width ];
05938                     QColor RGB(getR(RGB_uint),getG(RGB_uint),getB(RGB_uint));
05939                     pixel_text->setText(tr("img(")+QString::number(positionX+1)+","+QString::number(positionY+1)+") = "+"<font color="+RGB.name()+">"+"("+QString::number(getR(RGB_uint))+","+QString::number(getG(RGB_uint))+","+QString::number(getB(RGB_uint))+")");
05940                 }
05941 
05942             }
05943 
05944             if( image_disp == 2 ) {
05945 
05946                 const unsigned char* img1_filtered;
05947                 const unsigned int* img1_filtered_rgb;
05948 
05949                 QString img_str;
05950                 if( !hasPreprocess ) {
05951                     img_str = tr("img(");
05952                 }
05953                 else {
05954                     img_str = tr("img'(");
05955                 }
05956 
05957                 if( !isRgb1 ) {
05958                     img1_filtered = filters1->get_filtered();
05959                     int I = img1_filtered[positionX+positionY*img_width];
05960                     QColor RGB(I,I,I);
05961                     pixel_text->setText(img_str+QString::number(positionX+1)+","+QString::number(positionY+1)+") = "+"<font color="+RGB.name()+">"+QString::number(I));
05962                 }
05963 
05964                 else {
05965 
05966                     if( model == 1 ) {
05967                         img1_filtered_rgb = filtersRGB1->get_filtered();
05968 
05969                         unsigned int RGB_uint = img1_filtered_rgb[positionX+positionY*img_width];
05970                         QColor RGB(getR(RGB_uint),getG(RGB_uint),getB(RGB_uint));
05971 
05972                         pixel_text->setText(img_str+QString::number(positionX+1)+","+QString::number(positionY+1)+") = "+"<font color="+RGB.name()+">"+"("+QString::number(getR(RGB_uint))+","+QString::number(getG(RGB_uint))+","+QString::number(getB(RGB_uint))+")");
05973 
05974                     }
05975                     if( model == 2 ) {
05976                         img1_filtered = filtersRGB1->get_gradient();
05977 
05978                         int I = img1_filtered[ positionX+positionY*img_width ];
05979                         QColor RGB(I,I,I);
05980                         pixel_text->setText(img_str+QString::number(positionX+1)+","+QString::number(positionY+1)+") = "+"<font color="+RGB.name()+">"+QString::number(I));
05981 
05982                     }
05983 
05984                 }
05985             }
05986 
05987             show_phi_list_value();
05988 
05989         }
05990 
05991     }
05992 }

05994 inline void ImageViewer::show_phi_list_value() {
05995 
05996     const char* phi = NULL;
05997 
05998     if( !isRgb1 ) {
05999 
06000         if( model == 1 ) {
06001             if( acWithoutEdges1 != NULL ) {
06002                 phi = acWithoutEdges1->get_phi();
06003             }
06004         }
06005 
06006         if( model == 2 ) {
06007             if( geodesicAc1 != NULL ) {
06008                 phi = geodesicAc1->get_phi();
06009             }
06010         }
06011 
06012     }
06013 
06014     else {
06015 
06016         if( model == 1 ) {
06017             if( acWithoutEdgesYUV1 != NULL ) {
06018                 phi = acWithoutEdgesYUV1->get_phi();
06019             }
06020         }
06021 
06022         if( model == 2 ) {
06023             if( geodesicAc1 != NULL ) {
06024                 phi = geodesicAc1->get_phi();
06025             }
06026         }
06027     }
06028 
06029     if( phi != NULL ) {
06030         QColor RGBout(Rout1,Gout1,Bout1);
06031         QColor RGBin(Rin1,Gin1,Bin1);
06032 
06033         if( phi[ positionX+positionY*img_width ] == 3 ) {
06034             phi_text->setText("Œ¶("+QString::number(positionX+1)+","+QString::number(positionY+1)+","+QString::number(iterations1)+") = "+"<font color="+RGBout.name()+">"+QString::number(phi[positionX+positionY*img_width]));
06035             lists_text->setText("("+QString::number(positionX+1)+","+QString::number(positionY+1)+","+QString::number(iterations1)+") ‚àâ "+"<font color="+RGBout.name()+">"+"Lout"+"<font color=black>"+" & ‚àâ "+"<font color="+RGBin.name()+">"+"Lin");
06036         }
06037         else if( phi[ positionX+positionY*img_width ] == -3 ){
06038             phi_text->setText("Œ¶("+QString::number(positionX+1)+","+QString::number(positionY+1)+","+QString::number(iterations1)+") = "+"<font color="+RGBin.name()+">"+QString::number(phi[positionX+positionY*img_width]));
06039             lists_text->setText("("+QString::number(positionX+1)+","+QString::number(positionY+1)+","+QString::number(iterations1)+") ‚àâ "+"<font color="+RGBin.name()+">"+"Lin"+"<font color=black>"+" & ‚àâ "+"<font color="+RGBout.name()+">"+"Lout");
06040         }
06041 
06042         else if( phi[ positionX+positionY*img_width ] == 1 ) {
06043             phi_text->setText("Œ¶("+QString::number(positionX+1)+","+QString::number(positionY+1)+","+QString::number(iterations1)+") = "+"<font color="+RGBout.name()+">"+QString::number(phi[positionX+positionY*img_width]));
06044             lists_text->setText("("+QString::number(positionX+1)+","+QString::number(positionY+1)+","+QString::number(iterations1)+") ‚àà "+"<font color="+RGBout.name()+">"+"Lout");
06045         }
