06062 bool ImageViewer::eventFilter(QObject *object, QEvent *event)
06063 {
06064     // deplacement uniquement en fonction de imageLabel et pas main_window
06065     if( object == imageLabel && event->type() == QEvent::MouseMove ) {
06066         QMouseEvent* mouseEvent = static_cast<QMouseEvent*>(event);
06067         mouseMoveEvent(mouseEvent);
06068     }
06069 
06070     // pour avoir les ev√©nements keyPress
06071     if( object == imageLabel && event->type() == QEvent::KeyPress ) {
06072         QKeyEvent* keyEvent = static_cast<QKeyEvent*>(event);
06073         keyPressEvent(keyEvent);
06074     }
06075 
06076     // pour avoir les ev√©nements keyRelease
06077     if( object == imageLabel && event->type() == QEvent::KeyRelease ) {
06078         QKeyEvent* keyEvent = static_cast<QKeyEvent*>(event);
06079         keyReleaseEvent(keyEvent);
06080     }
06081 
06082     // clic pris en compte que sur la zone de imageLabel
06083     if( object == imageLabel && event->type() == QEvent::MouseButtonPress ) {
06084         QMouseEvent* mouseEvent = static_cast<QMouseEvent*>(event);
06085         mousePressEvent(mouseEvent);
06086     }
06087 
06088     // clic pris en compte que sur la zone de imageLabel
06089     if( object == imageLabel && event->type() == QEvent::MouseButtonRelease ) {
06090         QMouseEvent* mouseEvent = static_cast<QMouseEvent*>(event);
06091         mouseReleaseEvent(mouseEvent);
06092     }
06093 
06094     // molette prise en compte que sur la zone de imageLabel
06095     if( object == imageLabel && event->type() == QEvent::Wheel && (img1 != NULL || img1_rgb != NULL) ) {
06096         imageLabel->set_hasText(false);
06097         imageLabel->setBackgroundRole(QPalette::Dark);
06098         disconnect(scrollArea->verticalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustVerticalScroll (int,int)));
06099         disconnect(scrollArea->horizontalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustHorizontalScroll(int,int)));
06100         scale_spin0->setValue(int(100.0f*imageLabel->get_zoomFactor()));
06101         connect(scrollArea->verticalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustVerticalScroll (int,int)));
06102         connect(scrollArea->horizontalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustHorizontalScroll(int,int)));
06103     }
06104 
06105     if( (object == scale_spin0 || object == scale_slider0 || object == scale_spin || object == scale_slider) && event->type() == QEvent::MouseButtonPress ) {
06106         if( img1 != NULL || img1_rgb != NULL ) {
06107             imageLabel->set_hasText(false);
06108             imageLabel->setBackgroundRole(QPalette::Dark);
06109             imageLabel_settings->set_hasText(false);
06110             imageLabel_settings->setBackgroundRole(QPalette::Dark);
06111         }
06112         positionX = img_width/2;
06113         positionY = img_height/2;
06114     }
06115 
06116 
06117     // deplacement uniquement en fonction de imageLabel_settings et pas settings_window
06118     if( object == imageLabel_settings && event->type() == QEvent::MouseMove ) {
06119         QMouseEvent* mouseEvent = static_cast<QMouseEvent*>(event);
06120         mouseMoveEvent2(mouseEvent);
06121     }
06122 
06123     // clic pris en compte que sur la zone de imageLabel_settings
06124     if( object == imageLabel_settings && event->type() == QEvent::MouseButtonPress ) {
06125         QMouseEvent* mouseEvent = static_cast<QMouseEvent*>(event);
06126         mousePressEvent2(mouseEvent);
06127     }
06128 
06129     // molette prise en compte que sur la zone de imageLabel_settings
06130     if( object == imageLabel_settings && event->type() == QEvent::Wheel && (img1 != NULL || img1_rgb != NULL) ) {
06131         imageLabel_settings->set_hasText(false);
06132         imageLabel_settings->setBackgroundRole(QPalette::Dark);
06133         disconnect(scrollArea->verticalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustVerticalScroll (int,int)));
06134         disconnect(scrollArea->horizontalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustHorizontalScroll(int,int)));
06135         scale_spin->setValue(int(100.0f*imageLabel_settings->get_zoomFactor()));
06136         connect(scrollArea->verticalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustVerticalScroll (int,int)));
06137         connect(scrollArea->horizontalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustHorizontalScroll(int,int)));
06138         QWheelEvent* mouseEvent = static_cast<QWheelEvent*>(event);
06139         wheelEvent(mouseEvent);
06140     }
06141 
06142     if( object == scale_spinA && event->type() == QEvent::MouseButtonPress ) {
06143         if( !image1.isNull() ) {
06144             imageLabelA->set_hasText(false);
06145             imageLabelA->setBackgroundRole(QPalette::Dark);
06146         }
06147         positionXa = imgA_width/2;
06148         positionYa = imgA_height/2;
06149     }
06150 
06151     if( object == scale_spinB && event->type() == QEvent::MouseButtonPress ) {
06152         if( !image2.isNull() ) {
06153             imageLabelB->set_hasText(false);
06154             imageLabelB->setBackgroundRole(QPalette::Dark);
06155         }
06156         positionXb = imgB_width/2;
06157         positionYb = imgB_height/2;
06158     }
06159 
06160     // deplacement uniquement en fonction de imageLabelA
06161     if( object == imageLabelA && event->type() == QEvent::MouseMove ) {
06162         QMouseEvent* mouseEvent = static_cast<QMouseEvent*>(event);
06163         mouseMoveEventA(mouseEvent);
06164     }
06165     // clic pris en compte que sur la zone de imageLabelA
06166     if( object == imageLabelA && event->type() == QEvent::MouseButtonPress ) {
06167         QMouseEvent* mouseEvent = static_cast<QMouseEvent*>(event);
06168         mousePressEventA(mouseEvent);
06169     }
06170 
06171     if( object == imageLabelA && event->type() == QEvent::Wheel && !image1.isNull() ) {
06172         imageLabelA->set_hasText(false);
06173         imageLabelA->setBackgroundRole(QPalette::Dark);
06174         disconnect(scrollAreaA->verticalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustVerticalScrollA (int,int)));
06175         disconnect(scrollAreaA->horizontalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustHorizontalScrollA(int,int)));
06176         scale_spinA->setValue(int(100.0f*imageLabelA->get_zoomFactor()));
06177         connect(scrollAreaA->verticalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustVerticalScrollA (int,int)));
06178         connect(scrollAreaA->horizontalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustHorizontalScrollA(int,int)));
06179     }
06180 
06181     if( object == imageLabelB && event->type() == QEvent::Wheel && !image2.isNull() ) {
06182         imageLabelB->set_hasText(false);
06183         imageLabelB->setBackgroundRole(QPalette::Dark);
06184         disconnect(scrollAreaB->verticalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustVerticalScrollB (int,int)));
06185         disconnect(scrollAreaB->horizontalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustHorizontalScrollB(int,int)));
06186         scale_spinB->setValue(int(100.0f*imageLabelB->get_zoomFactor()));
06187         connect(scrollAreaB->verticalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustVerticalScrollB (int,int)));
06188         connect(scrollAreaB->horizontalScrollBar(),SIGNAL(rangeChanged(int,int)),this,SLOT(adjustHorizontalScrollB(int,int)));
06189     }
06190 
06191     // deplacement uniquement en fonction de imageLabelB
06192     if( object == imageLabelB && event->type() == QEvent::MouseMove ) {
06193         QMouseEvent* mouseEvent = static_cast<QMouseEvent*>(event);
06194         mouseMoveEventB(mouseEvent);
06195     }
06196     // clic pris en compte que sur la zone de imageLabelB
06197     if( object == imageLabelB && event->type() == QEvent::MouseButtonPress ) {
06198         QMouseEvent* mouseEvent = static_cast<QMouseEvent*>(event);
06199         mousePressEventB(mouseEvent);
06200     }
06201 
06202 
06203     if( object == imageLabel && event->type() == QEvent::DragEnter ) {
06204         QDragEnterEvent* drag = static_cast<QDragEnterEvent*>(event);
06205         dragEnterEvent(drag);
06206     }
06207     if( object == imageLabel && event->type() == QEvent::DragMove ) {
06208         QDragMoveEvent* drag = static_cast<QDragMoveEvent*>(event);
06209         dragMoveEvent(drag);
06210     }
06211     if( object == imageLabel && event->type() == QEvent::Drop ) {
06212         QDropEvent* drag = static_cast<QDropEvent*>(event);
06213         dropEvent(drag);
06214     }
06215     if( object == imageLabel && event->type() == QEvent::DragLeave ) {
06216         QDragLeaveEvent* drag = static_cast<QDragLeaveEvent*>(event);
06217         dragLeaveEvent(drag);
06218     }
06219 
06220     if( object == imageLabel_settings && event->type() == QEvent::DragEnter ) {
06221         QDragEnterEvent* drag = static_cast<QDragEnterEvent*>(event);
06222         dragEnterEventPhi(drag);
06223     }
06224     if( object == imageLabel_settings && event->type() == QEvent::DragMove ) {
06225         QDragMoveEvent* drag = static_cast<QDragMoveEvent*>(event);
06226         dragMoveEventPhi(drag);
06227     }
06228     if( object == imageLabel_settings && event->type() == QEvent::Drop ) {
06229         QDropEvent* drag = static_cast<QDropEvent*>(event);
06230         dropEventPhi(drag);
06231     }
06232     if( object == imageLabel_settings && event->type() == QEvent::DragLeave ) {
06233         QDragLeaveEvent* drag = static_cast<QDragLeaveEvent*>(event);
06234         dragLeaveEventPhi(drag);
06235     }
06236 
06237     if( object == imageLabelA && event->type() == QEvent::DragEnter ) {
06238         QDragEnterEvent* drag = static_cast<QDragEnterEvent*>(event);
06239         dragEnterEventA(drag);
06240     }
06241     if( object == imageLabelA && event->type() == QEvent::DragMove ) {
06242         QDragMoveEvent* drag = static_cast<QDragMoveEvent*>(event);
06243         dragMoveEventA(drag);
06244     }
06245     if( object == imageLabelA && event->type() == QEvent::Drop ) {
06246         QDropEvent* drag = static_cast<QDropEvent*>(event);
06247         dropEventA(drag);
06248     }
06249     if( object == imageLabelA && event->type() == QEvent::DragLeave ) {
06250         QDragLeaveEvent* drag = static_cast<QDragLeaveEvent*>(event);
06251         dragLeaveEventA(drag);
06252     }
06253 
06254     if( object == imageLabelB && event->type() == QEvent::DragEnter ) {
06255         QDragEnterEvent* drag = static_cast<QDragEnterEvent*>(event);
06256         dragEnterEventB(drag);
06257     }
06258     if( object == imageLabelB && event->type() == QEvent::DragMove ) {
06259         QDragMoveEvent* drag = static_cast<QDragMoveEvent*>(event);
06260         dragMoveEventB(drag);
06261     }
06262     if( object == imageLabelB && event->type() == QEvent::Drop ) {
06263         QDropEvent* drag = static_cast<QDropEvent*>(event);
06264         dropEventB(drag);
06265     }
06266     if( object == imageLabelB && event->type() == QEvent::DragLeave ) {
06267         QDragLeaveEvent* drag = static_cast<QDragLeaveEvent*>(event);
06268         dragLeaveEventB(drag);
06269     }
06270 
06271     if( object == imageLabel && event->type() == QEvent::MouseMove && positionX >=0 && positionX < img_width && positionY >= 0 && positionY < img_height ) {
06272         setCursor(Qt::CrossCursor);
06273     }
06274     else {
06275         setCursor(Qt::ArrowCursor);
06276     }
06277 
06278     return false;
06279 }
06280 
06282 void ImageViewer::mouseMoveEvent2(QMouseEvent *event2)
06283 {
06284 
06285     // si l'image est charg√©e et si on est dans l'onglet initialisation
06286     if( img1 != NULL || img1_rgb != NULL ) {
06287 
06288         // position de la souris dans l'image
06289         positionX = int(double(img_width)*double(   (  (event2->pos()).x() -imageLabel_settings->get_xoffset()   ) /double(imageLabel_settings->getPixWidth())));
06290         positionY = int(double(img_height)*double(   (  (event2->pos()).y() -imageLabel_settings->get_yoffset()   ) /double(imageLabel_settings->getPixHeight())));
06291 
06292         if( onglets->currentIndex()==1 ) {
06293 
06294             // on en deduit les valeurs relatives des sliders en %
06295 
06296             double a = (double(positionX)-double(img_width/2))/double(img_width);
06297             double b = (double(positionY)-double(img_height/2))/double(img_height);
06298 
06299             abscissa_spin->setValue(int(a*100.0));
06300             ordinate_spin->setValue(int(b*100.0));
06301 
06302         }
06303     }
06304 
06305 }
06306 
06307 
06308 
06310 void ImageViewer::mousePressEvent2(QMouseEvent *event2) {
06311 
06312     // si on est dans l'onglet d'initilisation
06313     if( (img1 != NULL || img1_rgb != NULL) && onglets->currentIndex() == 1 ) {
06314 
06315         // clic gauche, on ajoute une forme
06316         if (event2->button() == Qt::LeftButton) {
06317             add_visu();
06318         }
06319         // clic droit, on soustraie
06320         if (event2->button() == Qt::RightButton) {
06321             subtract_visu();
06322         }
06323         // clic du milieu, on change un rectangle en ellipse ou vice versa
06324         if (event2->button() == Qt::MidButton) {
06325             if( !rectangle_radio->isChecked() ) {
06326                 rectangle_radio->setChecked(true);
06327             }
06328             else {
06329                 ellipse_radio->setChecked(true);
06330             }
06331             shape_visu();
06332         }
06333 
06334     }
06335 
06336     // pour cacher ou non au clic gauche le contour actif initial quand on est dans l'onglet Preprocessing
06337     if( (img1 != NULL || img1_rgb != NULL) && onglets->currentIndex() == 2 ) {
06338         if( event2->button() == Qt::RightButton ) {
06339             if( hasContoursHidden ) {
06340                 hasContoursHidden = false;
06341             }
06342             else {
06343                 hasContoursHidden = true;
06344             }
06345             phi_visu(false);
06346         }
06347         if( event2->button() == Qt::LeftButton ) {
06348             hasContoursHidden = true;
06349             if( hasShowImg1 ) {
06350                 hasShowImg1 = false;
06351                 img1_visu();
06352             }
06353             else {
06354                 hasShowImg1 = true;
06355                 phi_visu(false);
06356             }
06357 
06358         }
06359     }
06360 
06361  }
06362 
06364 void ImageViewer::img1_visu()
06365 {
06366     if( img1 != NULL || img1_rgb != NULL ) {
06367 
06368         imageLabel_settings->set_qimage(img);
06369     }
06370 }
06371 
06373 void ImageViewer::wheelEvent(QWheelEvent *event)
06374 {
06375 
06376     // si une image est d√©ja charg√©e et si on est dans l'onglet d'initialisation
06377     if( (img1 != NULL || img1_rgb != NULL) && onglets->currentIndex() == 1 ) {
06378 
06379 
06380         // nombre de degr√© et de pas de la molette
06381         int numDegrees = event->delta() / 8;
06382         int numSteps = numDegrees / 15;
06383 
06384         // r√©cup√©ration des valeurs des sliders concernant la taille de la forme
06385         int width_ratio = width_shape_spin->value();
06386         int height_ratio = height_shape_spin->value();
06387 
06388         // correpondance par rapport √  la taille r√©elle de la forme
06389         double width = double(img_width)*double(width_ratio)/100.0;
06390         double height = double(img_height)*double(height_ratio)/100.0;
06391 
06392         // augmentation ou diminution de 15% √  chaque pas de molette
06393         width += 0.15*double(numSteps)*width;
06394         height += 0.15*double(numSteps)*height;
06395 
06396         width_ratio = int( round(100.0*width/double(img_width)) );
06397         height_ratio = int( round(100.0*height/double(img_height)) );
06398 
06399         if( (width_ratio > 3) && (height_ratio > 3) && (width_ratio < 150) && (height_ratio < 150) )  {
06400             width_shape_spin->setValue(width_ratio);
06401             height_shape_spin->setValue(height_ratio);
06402         }
06403 
06404         event->accept();
06405     }
06406

06442 void ImageViewer::open_imageA() {

06448             QMessageBox::information(this, tr("Ofeli Viewer"),
06449                                      tr("Cannot load %1.").arg(fileNameA));
06450             return;
06451         }
06452

06454         QApplication::processEvents();
06455 
06456         imgA_height = image1.height();
06457         imgA_width = image1.width();
06458         imgA_size = imgA_width*imgA_height;
06459 
06460         positionXa = imgA_width/2;
06461         positionYa = imgA_height/2;
06462 
06463         QFileInfo fi1(fileNameA);
06464         QString name1 = fi1.fileName();
06465 
06466         QString string_lists_text;
06467         string_lists_text=QString::number(imgA_width)+"√ó"+QString::number(imgA_height);

06469     }

06625 // calcule et affiche les distances d'Hausdorff et Hausdorff modifi√©e
06626 void ImageViewer::compute(int index) {
06627 
06628     if( index == 1 ) {
06629 
06630         // les deux pointeurs doivent point√©s sur un espace m√©moire allou√©
06631         if( !image1.isNull() && !image2.isNull() ) {
06632 
06633 
06634             // on r√©cup√®re les deux couleurs de chaque liste a partir des deux widgets de la fen√™tre d'√©valuation
06635 
06636             // les listes des points seront constitu√©s de la position des pixels ayant ces couleurs
06637 
06638             unsigned char redA;
06639             unsigned char greenA;
06640             unsigned char blueA;
06641 
06642             if( Acolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 0 ) {
06643                 redA = 255;
06644                 greenA = 0;
06645                 blueA = 0;
06646             }
06647             if( Acolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 1 ) {
06648                 redA = 0;
06649                 greenA = 255;
06650                 blueA = 0;
06651             }
06652             if( Acolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 2 ) {
06653                 redA = 0;
06654                 greenA = 0;
06655                 blueA = 255;
06656             }
06657             if( Acolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 3 ) {
06658                 redA = 0;
06659                 greenA = 255;
06660                 blueA = 255;
06661             }
06662             if( Acolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 4 ) {
06663                 redA = 255;
06664                 greenA = 0;
06665                 blueA = 255;
06666             }
06667             if( Acolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 5 ) {
06668                 redA = 255;
06669                 greenA = 255;
06670                 blueA = 0;
06671             }
06672             if( Acolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 6 ) {
06673                 redA = 0;
06674                 greenA = 0;
06675                 blueA = 0;
06676             }
06677             if( Acolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 7 ) {
06678                 redA = 255;
06679                 greenA = 255;
06680                 blueA = 255;
06681             }
06682             if( Acolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 8 ) {
06683                 redA = redAselected;
06684                 greenA = greenAselected;
06685                 blueA = blueAselected;
06686             }
06687 
06688             unsigned char redB;
06689             unsigned char greenB;
06690             unsigned char blueB;
06691 
06692             if( Bcolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 0 ) {
06693                 redB = 255;
06694                 greenB = 0;
06695                 blueB = 0;
06696             }
06697             if( Bcolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 1 ) {
06698                 redB = 0;
06699                 greenB = 255;
06700                 blueB = 0;
06701             }
06702             if( Bcolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 2 ) {
06703                 redB = 0;
06704                 greenB = 0;
06705                 blueB = 255;
06706             }
06707             if( Bcolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 3 ) {
06708                 redB = 0;
06709                 greenB =255;
06710                 blueB = 255;
06711             }
06712             if( Bcolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 4 ) {
06713                 redB = 255;
06714                 greenB = 0;
06715                 blueB = 255;
06716             }
06717             if( Bcolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 5 ) {
06718                 redB = 255;
06719                 greenB = 255;
06720                 blueB = 0;
06721             }
06722             if( Bcolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 6 ) {
06723                 redB = 0;
06724                 greenB = 0;
06725                 blueB = 0;
06726             }
06727             if( Bcolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 7 ) {
06728                 redB = 255;
06729                 greenB = 255;
06730                 blueB = 255;
06731             }
06732             if( Bcolor_combobox->currentIndex() == 8 ) {
06733                 redB = redBselected;
06734                 greenB = greenBselected;
06735                 blueB = blueBselected;
06736             }
06737 
06738 
06739             // d√©termination de la taille des listes
06740 
06741             int listA_length = 0;
06742             int listB_length = 0;
06743 
06744             QRgb pix;
06745             int x;
06746             int y;
06747 
06748             for( int i = 0; i < imgA_size; i++ ) {
06749 
06750                 // i = x+y*imgA_width so
06751                 y = i/imgA_width;
06752                 x = i-y*imgA_width;
06753 
06754                 pix = image1.pixel(x,y);
06755 
06756                 if( (unsigned char)(qRed(pix))==redA && (unsigned char)(qGreen(pix))==greenA && (unsigned char)(qBlue(pix)==blueA) ) {
06757                     listA_length++;
06758                 }
06759 
06760             }
06761 
06762             for( int i = 0; i < imgB_size; i++ ) {
06763 
06764                 // i = x+y*imgB_width so
06765                 y = i/imgB_width;
06766                 x = i-y*imgB_width;
06767 
06768                 pix = image2.pixel(x,y);
06769 
06770                 if( (unsigned char)(qRed(pix)) == redB && (unsigned char)(qGreen(pix)) == greenB && (unsigned char)(qBlue(pix) == blueB) ) {
06771                     listB_length++;
06772                 }
06773 
06774             }
06775 
06776             // on d√©clare les pointeurs et alloue la m√©moire de chaque liste en fonction de leur taille
06777 
06778             int* listA = new int[listA_length];
06779             int* listB = new int[listB_length];
06780 
06781 
06782             // on remplit les listes
06783 
06784             int index1 = 0;
06785             int index2=0;
06786 
06787             for( int i = 0; i < imgA_size; i++ ) {
06788 
06789                 y = i/imgA_width;
06790                 x = i-y*imgA_width;
06791 
06792                 pix = image1.pixel(x,y);
06793 
06794                 if( (unsigned char)(qRed(pix)) == redA && (unsigned char)(qGreen(pix)) == greenA && (unsigned char)(qBlue(pix) == blueA) ) {
06795                     listA[index1] = i;
06796                     index1++;
06797                 }
06798             }
06799 
06800             for( int i = 0; i < imgB_size; i++ ) {
06801 
06802                 y = i/imgB_width;
06803                 x = i-y*imgB_width;
06804 
06805                 pix = image2.pixel(x,y);
06806 
06807                 if( (unsigned char)(qRed(pix)) == redB && (unsigned char)(qGreen(pix)) == greenB && (unsigned char)(qBlue(pix) == blueB) ) {
06808                     listB[index2] = i;
06809                     index2++;
06810                 }
06811             }
06812 
06813 
06814             // cr√©ation d'un objet a partir des listes
06815             ofeli::HausdorffDistance hausdorffDistance1(listA, listA_length, imgA_width, imgA_height, listB, listB_length, imgB_width, imgB_height);
06816 
06817             // utilisation des accesseurs
06818             double hausdorff_dist1 = hausdorffDistance1.get_hausdorff_dist();
06819             double modified_hausdorff_dist1 = hausdorffDistance1.get_modified_hausdorff_dist();
06820             double hausdorff_ratio1 = hausdorffDistance1.get_hausdorff_ratio();
06821             double modified_hausdorff_ratio1 = hausdorffDistance1.get_modified_hausdorff_ratio();
06822             double centers_dist1 = hausdorffDistance1.get_centers_dist();
06823             double centers_ratio1 = hausdorffDistance1.get_centers_ratio();
06824 
06825             // affichage
06826             if( listA_length != 0 && listB_length != 0 ) {
06827                 label_hausdorff->setText(tr("Hausdorff distance = ")+QString::number(hausdorff_dist1)+(tr(" pixels")));
06828                 label_hausdorff_ratio->setText(tr("Hausdorff ratio = ")+QString::number(100.0*hausdorff_ratio1)+(" %"));
06829                 label_modified_hausdorff->setText(tr("modified Hausdorff distance = ")+QString::number(modified_hausdorff_dist1)+(tr(" pixels")));
06830                 label_modified_hausdorff_ratio->setText(tr("modified Hausdorff ratio = ")+QString::number(100.0*modified_hausdorff_ratio1)+(" %"));
06831                 label_centers_dist->setText(tr("distance between centers = ")+QString::number(centers_dist1)+(tr(" pixels")));
06832                 label_centers_ratio->setText(tr("ratio between centers = ")+QString::number(100.0*centers_ratio1)+(" %"));
06833             }
06834             else {
06835                 QString error_msg1;
06836                 QString error_msg2;
06837                 if( listA_length == 0 && listB_length == 0 ) {
06838                     error_msg1 = (tr("Error. The lists A and B are empty."));
06839                     error_msg2 = (tr("Change the lists colors."));
06840                 }
06841                 if( listA_length == 0 && listB_length != 0 ) {
06842                     error_msg1 = (tr("Error. The list A is empty."));
06843                     error_msg2 = (tr("Change the list A color."));
06844                 }
06845                 if( listA_length != 0 && listB_length == 0 ) {
06846                     error_msg1 = (tr("Error. The list B is empty."));
06847                     error_msg2 = (tr("Change the list B color."));
06848                 }
06849 
06850                 label_hausdorff->setText(error_msg1);
06851                 label_hausdorff_ratio->setText(error_msg2);
06852                 label_modified_hausdorff->setText(error_msg1);
06853                 label_modified_hausdorff_ratio->setText(error_msg2);
06854                 label_centers_dist->setText(error_msg1);
06855                 label_centers_ratio->setText(error_msg2);
06856             }
06857 
06858             // on supprime les listes
06859             delete[] listA;
06860             delete[] listB;
06861         }
06862 
06863         else {
06864             QString error_msg1;
06865             QString error_msg2;
06866             if( image1.isNull() && image2.isNull() ) {
06867                 error_msg1 = (tr("Error. The images A and B are not open."));
06868                 error_msg2 = (tr("Open image A and image B."));
06869             }
06870             if( image1.isNull() && !image2.isNull() ) {
06871                 error_msg1 = (tr("Error. The image A is not open."));
06872                 error_msg2 = (tr("Open image A."));
06873             }
06874             if( !image1.isNull() && image2.isNull() ) {
06875                 error_msg1 = (tr("Error. The image B is not open."));
06876                 error_msg2 = (tr("Open image B."));
06877             }
06878 
06879             label_hausdorff->setText(error_msg1);
06880             label_hausdorff_ratio->setText(error_msg2);
06881             label_modified_hausdorff->setText(error_msg1);
06882             label_modified_hausdorff_ratio->setText(error_msg2);
06883             label_centers_dist->setText(error_msg1);
06884             label_centers_ratio->setText(error_msg2);
06885 
06886         }
06887 
06888     }
06889 }

06923 // Pour afficher une image en niveau de gris √  partir d'un pointeur sur buffer 8 bits
06924 /*
06925 image1=QImage(ptr_buffer_8bits, img_width, img_height, img_width, QImage::Format_Indexed8);
06926 QVector<QRgb> table(256);
06927 image1.setColorTable(table);

06932 imageLabel->setPixmap(pixmap1);

06935 
06936 inline unsigned char ImageViewer::getR(unsigned int RGB) {
06937     return RGB & 0xFF;
06938 }
06939 
06940 inline unsigned char ImageViewer::getG(unsigned int RGB) {
06941     return (RGB >> 8) & 0xFF;
06942 }
06943 
06944 inline unsigned char ImageViewer::getB(unsigned int RGB) {
06945     return (RGB >> 16) & 0xFF;
06946 }
06947 
06948 inline unsigned int ImageViewer::setRGB(unsigned char R, unsigned char G, unsigned char B) {
06949     RGB = 0x000000FF & (unsigned int)(R);
06950     RGB |= 0x0000FF00 & ( (unsigned int)(G) << 8 );
06951     RGB |= 0x00FF0000 & ( (unsigned int)(B) << 16 );
06952     return RGB;
06953 }
06954 
06955 void ImageViewer::dragEnterEvent(QDragEnterEvent *event)
06956 {
06957     if( !settings_window->isVisible() ) {
06958         QString text(tr("<drop image>"));
06959         imageLabel->set_text(text);
06960         imageLabel->setBackgroundRole(QPalette::Highlight);
06961         imageLabel->set_hasText(true);
06962 
06963         event->acceptProposedAction();
06964         emit changed(event->mimeData());
06965     }
06966 }
06967 
06968 void ImageViewer::dragMoveEvent(QDragMoveEvent *event)
06969 {
06970     if( !settings_window->isVisible() ) {
06971         event->acceptProposedAction();
06972     }
06973 }
06974 
06975 void ImageViewer::dropEvent(QDropEvent *event)
06976 {
06977     if( !settings_window->isVisible() ) {
06978 
06979         const QMimeData* mimeData = event->mimeData();
06980 
06981         if( mimeData->hasUrls() ) {
06982             QList<QUrl> urlList = mimeData->urls();
06983             fileName = urlList.first().toLocalFile();
06984         }
06985         imageLabel->setBackgroundRole(QPalette::Dark);
06986         open();
06987         event->acceptProposedAction();
06988     }
06989 
06990 }
06991

06993 {
06994     if( !settings_window->isVisible() ) {
06995         QString text(tr("<drag image>"));
06996         imageLabel->set_text(text);
06997         imageLabel->setBackgroundRole(QPalette::Dark);
06998         imageLabel->set_hasText(true);
06999         emit changed();
07000         event->accept();
07001     }
07002 }

07067 void ImageViewer::dropEventA(QDropEvent *event)
07068 {
07069     const QMimeData* mimeData = event->mimeData();
07070 
07071     if( mimeData->hasUrls() ) {

07186 void ImageViewer::open_phi() {
07187 
07188     if( img1 != NULL || img1_rgb != NULL ) {
07189 
07190         if( !fileName_phi.isEmpty() ) {
07191 
07192             QFileInfo fi(fileName_phi);
07193             last_directory_used = fi.absolutePath();
07194 
07195             QImage img_phi1 = QImage(fileName_phi);
07196 
07197             if( img_phi1.isNull() ) {
07198                 QMessageBox::information(this, tr("Ofeli Viewer"),
07199                                          tr("Cannot load %1.").arg(fileName_phi));
07200                 return;
07201             }
07202 
07203             img_phi1 = img_phi1.convertToFormat(QImage::Format_RGB888);
07204             img_phi1 = img_phi1.scaled(img_width, img_height, Qt::IgnoreAspectRatio, Qt::FastTransformation);
07205 
07206             QRgb pix;
07207             int x;
07208             int y;
07209 
07210             for( int i = 0; i < size1; i++ ) {
07211 
07212                 // i = x+y*img_width so
07213                 y = i/img_width;
07214                 x = i-y*img_width;
07215 
07216                 pix = img_phi1.pixel(x,y);
07217 
07218                 if( (0.2989*(double)(qRed(pix)) + 0.5870*(double)(qGreen(pix)) + 0.1140*(double)(qBlue(pix)) ) < 128.0 ) {
07219                     phi_init1[i] = 1;
07220                     phi_init2[i] = 1;
07221                 }
07222                 else {
07223                     phi_init1[i] = -1;
07224                     phi_init2[i] = -1;
07225                 }
07226 
07227             }
07228 
07229             clean_boundaries(phi_init1,phi_init1_clean);
07230             clean_boundaries(phi_init2,phi_init2_clean);
07231 
07232             QSettings settings;
07233 
07234             settings.setValue("Settings/Initialization/img_phi", img_phi1);
07235         }
07236 
07237         tab_visu(onglets->currentIndex());
07238     }
07239 }
07240 
07241 void ImageViewer::save_phi() {
07242 
07243     if( phi_init2_clean != NULL ) {
07244 
07245         QImage img_phi_save = QImage(img_width,img_height, QImage::Format_RGB888);
07246 
07247         int x;
07248         int y;
07249 
07250         for( int i = 0; i < size1; i++ ) {
07251 
07252             // i = x+y*img_width so
07253             y = i/img_width;
07254             x = i-y*img_width;
07255 
07256             if( phi_init2_clean[i] > 0 ) {
07257                 img_phi_save.setPixel(x,y,qRgb(0,0,0));
07258             }
07259             else {
07260                 img_phi_save.setPixel(x,y,qRgb(255,255,255));
07261             }
07262 
07263         }
07264 
07265         QString fileName_save = QFileDialog::getSaveFileName(this,
07266                                                              tr("Save Œ¶(t=0)"),
07267                                                              last_directory_used + QString(tr("/initial_phi.png")),
07268                                                              "PNG (*.png)");
07269         // sauvegarde
07270         img_phi_save.save(fileName_save);
07271 
07272     }
07273 }

07385 void ImageViewer::setCurrentFile(const QString &fileName1)
07386 {
07387     curFile = fileName1;
07388     //setWindowFilePath(curFile);
07389 
07390     QSettings settings;
07391     QStringList files = settings.value("name/recentFileList").toStringList();
07392     files.removeAll(fileName1);
07393     files.prepend(fileName1);
07394     while( files.size() > MaxRecentFiles )
07395         files.removeLast();
07396 
07397     settings.setValue("name/recentFileList", files);
07398 
07399     foreach( QWidget *widget, QApplication::topLevelWidgets() ) {
07400         ImageViewer *imageViewer = qobject_cast<ImageViewer *>(widget);
07401         if( imageViewer )
07402             imageViewer->updateRecentFileActions();
07403     }
07404 }
07405 
07406 void ImageViewer::updateRecentFileActions()
07407 {
07408     QSettings settings;
07409     QStringList files = settings.value("name/recentFileList").toStringList();
07410 
07411     int numRecentFiles = qMin(files.size(), (int)MaxRecentFiles);
07412 
07413     for( int i = 0; i < numRecentFiles; ++i ) {
07414         QString text = tr("&%1   %2").arg(i + 1).arg( strippedName(files[i]) );
07415         recentFileActs[i]->setText(text);
07416         recentFileActs[i]->setData(files[i]);
07417         recentFileActs[i]->setVisible(true);
07418     }
07419     for( int j = numRecentFiles; j < MaxRecentFiles; ++j )
07420         recentFileActs[j]->setVisible(false);
07421 
07422     separatorAct->setVisible(numRecentFiles > 0);
07423 
07424     if( files.isEmpty() ) {
07425         deleteAct->setVisible(false);
07426     }
07427     else {
07428         deleteAct->setVisible(true);
07429     }
07430 }
07431

07434     return QFileInfo(fullFileName).fileName();
07435 }

07446 void ImageViewer::deleteList()
07447 {
07448     QStringList files;
07449     files.clear();
07450 
07451     QSettings settings;
07452     settings.setValue("name/recentFileList", files);
